Section 1:
26 RS BR 1380
1 A JOINT RESOLUTION relating to road projects.
3 Section 1. Notwithstanding KRS 48.300, this Joint Resolution in conjunction with
4 2026 Regular Session HB 502 and 2026 Regular Session HJR 75 shall constitute the Six-
5 Year Road Plan. The Local Assistance Road Program projects are as follows:
